                  <hi rend="ital">He renewed his acquaintance with it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">his knowledge of it;</hi> (S, O, L, Msb, K;) this is the proper signification; (Msb;) as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30859-1" target="اعتهدهُ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>; (O, * L, K;) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30859-2" target="تعاهدهُ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30859"/></foreign>; (L, K;) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30859-3" target="عاهدهُ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">مُعَاهَدَةٌ</foreign>: (L:) and <hi rend="ital">he sought it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">sought for it</hi> or <hi rend="ital">after it, it being absent from him;</hi> syn. <foreign lang="ar">تَفَقَّدَهُ</foreign>; as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30859-4" target="تعاهدهُ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30859"/></foreign>, and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30859-5" target="اعتهده" n="5" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>: (K:) or <foreign lang="ar">تعهّدهُ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">تفقّدهُ</foreign> are used, by some, each in the place of the other; but accord. to Er-Rághib and many others, the former signifies <hi rend="ital">he sought,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">sought leisurely</hi> or <hi rend="ital">repeatedly, to obtain knowledge of it, having known of it before;</hi> and the latter, <hi rend="ital">he sought,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">sought leisurely</hi> or <hi rend="ital">repeatedly, to obtain knowledge of it, having lost it:</hi> (MF in art. <foreign lang="ar">فقد</foreign>:) or <foreign lang="ar">تعهّدهُ</foreign> signifies <hi rend="ital">he renewed his acquaintance with it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">his knowledge of it, and sought,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">sought leisurely</hi> or <hi rend="ital">repeatedly, to find means of rectifying it, reforming it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">putting it into a good</hi> or <hi rend="ital">right</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proper state:</hi> (IDrst, TA:) or <hi rend="ital">he came to it, and rectified it, reformed it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">put it into a good</hi> or <hi rend="ital">right</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proper state:</hi> (Mgh:) or as first expl. above, and also <hi rend="ital">he returned to it time after time,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">went frequently to it, and rectified it, reformed it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">put it into a good</hi> or <hi rend="ital">right</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proper state:</hi> (Msb:) or, simply, [as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30859-6" target="تعاهدهُ" n="6" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30859"/></foreign>,] <hi rend="ital">he returned,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">recurred, to it time after time,</hi> [see an instance voce <foreign lang="ar">أَخْرَقُ</foreign>,] or <hi rend="ital">went frequently to it:</hi> (Et-Tedmuree, TA:) and also [i. e. both signify also <hi rend="ital">he paid repeated,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">frequent, attention to it;</hi> or] <hi rend="ital">he was careful,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">mindful, of it;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">attentive to it.</hi> (S, O, Msb. *) One says also, <foreign lang="ar">تَعَهَّدْتُ فُلَانًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I renewed my acquaintance with such a one; repaired,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">betook myself, to him frequently; paid frequent attention to him;</hi> or simply <hi rend="ital">paid attention to him</hi>]. (S, O.) And <foreign lang="ar">تَعَهَّدْتُ ضَيْعَتِى</foreign>, (S, O, Mgh,) properly signifying <hi rend="ital">I renewed my acquaintance with,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">my knowledge of, my estate,</hi> is used as meaning <hi rend="ital">I came to my estate, and put it into a good</hi> or <hi rend="ital">right</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proper condition:</hi> (Mgh:) [or <hi rend="ital">I paid repeated,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">frequent,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">much, attention to it, taking good and effectual care of it; I husbanded it well:</hi>] or, accord. to IDrst, the verb here has the meaning given above on his authority: or, accord. to Ed-Tedmuree, the meaning is that given above as his explanation; and is from <foreign lang="ar">عَهْدٌ</foreign> as signifying “ rain that falls after other rain, ” or from the same word as signifying “ a place of abode in which one has known a thing: ” (TA:) and one may say also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30859-7" target="تَعَاهَدْتُ" n="7" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>; (Fr, ISk, Mgh;) but <foreign lang="ar">تَعَهَّدْتُ</foreign> is more chaste, (El-Fá- rábee, S, O, Msb,) because   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30859-8" target="تَعَاهُدٌ" n="8" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> is only between two [or more]: (S, O:) or <foreign lang="ar">تعاهدت</foreign> is not allowable, (AZ, AHát, Th, IF, Msb,) for the reason just mentioned: (IF, Msb:) AZ says that six Arabs of the desert, of chaste speech, being asked in the presence of himself and of Yoo, one after another, whether they said <foreign lang="ar">تعهّدت ضيعتى</foreign> or   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30859-9" target="تعاهدت" n="9" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30859"/></foreign>, all answered, <foreign lang="ar">تعهّدت</foreign>. (AHát, TA.) One also says, of a man, <foreign lang="ar">يَتَعَهَّدُهُ صَرْعٌ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Epilepsy befalls him repeatedly,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">time after time</hi>]. (S, O.)    </entryFree>29:T389d,<entryFree id="n30861" key="عَهْدٌ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">عَهْدٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form> [an inf. n. of 1, q. v.: used as a simple subst.,] <hi rend="ital">An injunction, a charge, a bidding, an order,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a command.</hi> (S, A, Mgh, O, Msb, K, TA.) [Pl. in this and other senses <foreign lang="ar">عُهُودٌ</foreign>.] <foreign lang="ar">عَهْدِى</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">أَنْ لَا آخُذَ مِنْ رَاضِعٍ شَيْئًا</foreign>, occurring in a trad., is a phrase tropically abridged, meaning <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">It is in the injunction,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">charge, prescribed as obligatory on me</hi> [<hi rend="ital">that I should not take anything from a suckling</hi>]. (Mgh.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">A compact, a contract, a covenant, an agreement, a confederacy, a league, a treaty, an engagement, a bond, an obligation,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a promise:</hi> (S, A, Mgh, O, L, Msb, K, TA:) pl. <foreign lang="ar">عُهُودٌ</foreign>: or, accord. to AHeyth,   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-1" target="عَهْدَةٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30863"/></foreign> has this this meaning, and <foreign lang="ar">عَهْدٌ</foreign> is its pl. [or rather a coll. gen. n.]. (TA.) Hence <foreign lang="ar">وَلِىُّ عَهْدٍ</foreign> The <hi rend="ital">suc-</hi> 
                  <pb n="2183"/> 
                  <hi rend="ital">cessor by virtue of a covenant</hi> of a Khaleefeh [or King]. (TA.) [And <foreign lang="ar">وِلَايَةُ عَهْدٍ</foreign> The <hi rend="ital">succession by virtue of a covenant.</hi>]          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">Protection,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">safeguard; a promise,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">an assurance, of security</hi> or <hi rend="ital">safety; responsibility,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">suretiship;</hi> syn. <foreign lang="ar">أَمَانٌ</foreign>; and <foreign lang="ar">ذِمَّةٌ</foreign>; (Sh, S, A, O, Msb, K;) and <foreign lang="ar">ضَمَانٌ</foreign>; (O, K;) as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-2" target="عُهَّيْدَى" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> [in the O   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-3" target="عُهَيْدَى" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30870"/></foreign>] and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-4" target="عِهْدَانٌ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30866"/></foreign> [which last is said in the S and O to be syn. with <foreign lang="ar">عَهْدٌ</foreign>, but in what sense is not there specified]. (K.) Hence, <foreign lang="ar">ذُو عَهْدٍ</foreign>, an appel-lation given to a Christian, and a Jew, [and a Sabian, who is a subject of a Muslim government,] meaning <hi rend="ital">One between whom and the Muslims a compact,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">covenant, subsists, whereby the latter are responsible for his security</hi> [<hi rend="ital">and freedom and toleration</hi>] <hi rend="ital">as long as he acts agreeably to the compact</hi> [<hi rend="ital">by living peaceably with them and paying a poll-tax</hi>]; (Mgh, * Msb, * TA;) [i. e. <hi rend="ital">a free non-Muslim subject of a Muslim government;</hi>] as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-5" target="مُعَاهِدٌ" n="5" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30874"/></foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-6" target="مُعَاهَدٌ" n="6" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, the act. and pass. forms being both applied to such a person because the compact is mutual; (Msb;) both syn. with <foreign lang="ar">ذِمِّىٌّ</foreign>: (S:) persons of this description are called collectively <foreign lang="ar">أَهْلُ العَهْدِ</foreign>. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">An oath:</hi> (S, A, O, K:) pl. <foreign lang="ar">عُهُودٌ</foreign>: or, accord. to AHeyth,   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-7" target="عَهْدَةٌ" n="7" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30863"/></foreign> signifies <hi rend="ital">an oath whereby one secures himself against him with whom he makes a compact, contract, covenant,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like,</hi> and <foreign lang="ar">عَهْدٌ</foreign> is its pl. [or rather a coll. gen. n.]. (TA.) [But it is generally used as a sing.: hence,] one says, <foreign lang="ar">عَلَىَّ عَهْدُ ٱللّٰهِ لَأَفْعَلَنَّ كَذَا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">The oath by attestation of God is binding on me that I will assuredly do such a thing</hi>]. (S, O.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">A writ,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">diploma, of appointment to the office of a prefect</hi> or <hi rend="ital">governor</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like:</hi> (S, O, K:) pl. <foreign lang="ar">عُهُودٌ</foreign>. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="6">-b6-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">Defence of those persons,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">things, that should be sacred,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">inviolable,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">that are entitled to reverence, respect, honour,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">defence;</hi> (S, A, O, K;) and <hi rend="ital">mindfulness, regard,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">observance,</hi> (S, K,) <hi rend="ital">of such things,</hi> (K,) or <hi rend="ital">of love,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">affection;</hi> occurring in this sense in a trad., in which it is said that generosity therein is a point of religion. (S.)          <sense type="b" n="7">-b7-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">Fulfilment of a promise</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like.</hi> (O, K.) So in the Kur vii. 100. (O.)          <sense type="b" n="8">-b8-</sense>  The <hi rend="ital">assertion of the unity of God:</hi> whence, <foreign lang="ar">إِلَّا</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">مَنِ ٱتَّخَذَ عِنْدَ ٱلرَّحْمٰنِ عَهْدًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Except such as hath made a covenant with the Compassionate to assert his unity</hi>], (O, K,) in the Kur [xix. 90]: (O:) and the words of a trad. relating to prayer, <foreign lang="ar">أَنَا</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">عَلَى عَهْدِكَ وَوَعْدِكَ مَا ٱسْتَطَعْتُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">I am persevering in the observance of my covenant and promise to Thee to believe in Thee and to assert thy unity incessantly</hi> [<hi rend="ital">as far as I am able</hi>]. (TA.)       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  Also <hi rend="ital">A time;</hi> (S, * A, K;) and so   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-8" target="عِهْدَانٌ" n="8" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30866"/></foreign>. (A, TA.) One says, <foreign lang="ar">كَانَ عَلَى عَهْدِ فُلَانٍ</foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-9" target="عِهْدَانِهِ" n="9" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">It was in the time of such a one.</hi> (A.) And <foreign lang="ar">كَانَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">ذٰلِكَ فِى عَهْدِ شَبَابِى</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">That was in the time of my youth,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">young manhood.</hi> (TK.) And <foreign lang="ar">أَتَى عَلَيْهَا</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">عَهْدٌ طَوِيلٌ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Over which a long time has passed</hi>]. (S, in explanation of <foreign lang="ar">قَرْيَةٌ عَهِيدَةٌ</foreign> meaning <foreign lang="ar">قَدِيمَةٌ</foreign>.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  One says also, <foreign lang="ar">عَهْدِى بِهِ قَرِيبٌ</foreign> i. e. <hi rend="ital">My meeting</hi> [<hi rend="ital">with him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, was a short time ago</hi>]. (S, * Msb.) And <foreign lang="ar">هُوَ قَرِيبُ العَهْدِ بَكَذَا</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He knew,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">was acquainted with, such a thing,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">was in such a state,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">condition, recently,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a short time ago.</hi> (Msb. [And in like manner one says <foreign lang="ar">حَدِيثُ العَهْدِ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">حَدِيثُ عَهْدٍ</foreign>.]) And <foreign lang="ar">عَهْدِى بِهِ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">بِمَوْضِعِ كَذَا</foreign>, (K, TA,) and <foreign lang="ar">فِى حَالِ كَذَا</foreign>, (TA,) <hi rend="ital">I met,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">met with,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">I knew,</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">I saw,</hi>] <hi rend="ital">him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, in such a place,</hi> (K, TA,) and <hi rend="ital">in such a state,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">condition.</hi> (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">مَا لِى عَهْدٌ بِهِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I have not any knowledge of,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">acquaintance with, him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it</hi>]. (A.) And <foreign lang="ar">مَتَى عَهْدُكَ بِفُلَانٍ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">When didst thou meet,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">meet with, such a one?</hi> (Mgh:) or <hi rend="ital">see such a one?</hi> (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">مَتَى عَهْدُكَ بِالخُفِّ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">When didst thou wear the boots?</hi> (Mgh.) And <foreign lang="ar">مَتَى عَهْدُكَ بِأَسْفَلِ فِيكَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">When didst thou see the lower part of thy mouth?</hi>]: a prov.; said in asking a person respecting an old affair of which he has no knowledge. (L.) The saying of the poet, (Aboo-Khirásh El-Hudhalee, TA, and so in a copy of the S,) <quote>
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">فَلَيْسَ كَعَهْدِ الدَّارِ يَا أُمَّ مَالِكٍ</foreign>
                     </L> 
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">وَلٰكِنْ أَحَاطَتْ بِالرِّقَابِ السَّلَاسِلُ</foreign>
                     </L> 
                  </quote> [<hi rend="ital">And it is not like the formerly-known state of the abode, O Umm-Málik; but chains have surrounded the necks;</hi>] is expl. as meaning, the case is not as thou knewest it; but El-Islám has come, and has subverted that case. (S, TA.) [Hence, <foreign lang="ar">لِلْعَهْدِ</foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-10" target="لِلْمَعْهُودِ" n="10" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, said of the article <foreign lang="ar">اَلْ</foreign>; meaning <hi rend="ital">Used to distinguish a noun as known to the hearer,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">reader, in a particular sense.</hi>]       <sense type="A" n="3">-A3-</sense>  Also <hi rend="ital">A first rain;</hi> the rain immediately following which is called <foreign lang="ar">وَلْىٌ</foreign>: (TA:) or the <hi rend="ital">first of the rain called</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الوَسْمِىُّ</foreign>; (IAar, M, K;) and so   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-11" target="عَهْدَةٌ" n="11" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30863"/></foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-12" target="عِهْدَةٌ" n="12" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30865"/></foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-13" target="عِهَادَةٌ" n="13" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30869"/></foreign>, (M, K, TA,) or, as in some copies of the K [and in the CK],   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-14" target="عِهَادٌ" n="14" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30867"/></foreign>, which is pl. of <foreign lang="ar">عَهْدٌ</foreign>. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  And <hi rend="ital">Rain that falls after other rain,</hi> (AHn, S, K,) <hi rend="ital">while the moisture of the former yet remains;</hi> (AHn, K;) as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-15" target="عَهْدَةٌ" n="15" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30863"/></foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30861-16" target="عِهْدَةٌ" n="16" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30865"/></foreign>: (TA:) pl. <foreign lang="ar">عِهَادٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">عُهُودٌ</foreign>: (S:) or <foreign lang="ar">عِهَادٌ</foreign>, accord. to some, signifies <hi rend="ital">recent rains;</hi> app. from the saying, <foreign lang="ar">أَصَابَتْنَا دِيمَةٌ بِعْدَ دِيمَةٍ عَلَى عِهَادٍ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">غَيْرِ قَدِيمَةٍ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">A continuous and still rain fell upon us after a continuous and still rain following upon</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">عهاد</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">not long anterior</hi>]: (AHn, TA:) or <foreign lang="ar">عِهَادٌ</foreign> signifies <hi rend="ital">rains of the</hi> [<hi rend="ital">season called</hi>] <foreign lang="ar">رَبِيع</foreign> [here meaning <hi rend="ital">autumn,</hi> as is shown voce <foreign lang="ar">نَوْءٌ</foreign>], <hi rend="ital">after the rain called</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الوَسْمِىّ</foreign>: (A:) or <hi rend="ital">weak, fine rain, of that which is called</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">وَسْمِىّ</foreign>. (IAar, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">عَامُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">العُهُودِ</foreign> means <hi rend="ital">The year of few rains.</hi> (TA.)       <sense type="A" n="4">-A4-</sense>  See also <foreign lang="ar">عُهْدَةٌ</foreign>, near the middle, in two places:       <sense type="A" n="5">-A5-</sense>  and see <foreign lang="ar">مَعْهَدٌ</foreign>, in three places.    </entryFree>2a:T468,<entryFree id="n30863" key="عَهْدَةٌ" type="main">

                  </form>: see <foreign lang="ar">عَهْدٌ</foreign>, former half, in two places:       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  and again, in the last quarter, in two places.       <sense type="A" n="3">-A3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">عهدة</foreign> [thus written, without any syll. sign], in a verse cited by AHeyth, [the measure of which shows it to be <foreign lang="ar">عَهْدَةٌ</foreign> or   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30863-1" target="عُهْدَةٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30864"/></foreign> or

                  </form> 
                  <hi rend="ital">A written statement of a purchase</hi> or <hi rend="ital">sale:</hi> (S, Msb, K:) so called because one recurs to it on an occasion of doubt. (Msb.) And <hi rend="ital">A written statement of a confederacy, league, compact,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">covenant.</hi> (K.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  Also <hi rend="ital">A return</hi> [to claim an indemnification for a fault or the like in a thing purchased]; syn. <foreign lang="ar">رَجْعَةٌ</foreign>: so in the saying, <foreign lang="ar">لَا عُهْدَةَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">There shall be no return</hi> to claim an indemnification]: (S, O, K:) one says, <foreign lang="ar">أَبِيعُكَ المَلَسَى لَا عُهْدَةَ</foreign> i. e. [<hi rend="ital">I sell to thee on the condition that</hi>] <hi rend="ital">thou shalt get thee away, and not return to me,</hi> (S in this art., and S and Msb and K in art. <foreign lang="ar">ملس</foreign>,) <hi rend="ital">nor have any claim upon me for indemnification:</hi> (Msb in art. <foreign lang="ar">ملس</foreign>:) <foreign lang="ar">عُهْدَةٌ</foreign> with respect to an article of merchandise being when it is sold in a faulty state or subject to a claim on the part of its owner. (TA. [See more voce <foreign lang="ar">مَلَسَى</foreign>.]) One says also, <foreign lang="ar">عَلَيْكَ فِى</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">هٰذِهِ عُهْدَةٌ لَا تَتَفَصَّى مِنْهَا</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">Thou art subject to a claim for acting unjustly</hi> [<hi rend="ital">in respect of this, from which thou wilt not liberate thyself</hi>]. (A, TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">عُهْدَةُ الرَّقِيقِ ثَلَاثَةُ أَيَّامٍ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The claim for indemnification for a fault in a slave, from the property of the seller, if he have sold him without making it a condition that he is clear of responsibility for any fault, is during three days,</hi> and the purchaser may return him without proof; but if he find a fault after three days, he may not return him without proof. (TA, from a trad.) And   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n30864-1" target="عَهْدٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n30861"/></foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">عُهْدَةٌ</foreign> signify the same: (TA:) you say, <foreign lang="ar">بَرِئْتُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">إِلَيْكَ مِنْ عُهْدَةِ هٰذَا العَبْدِ</foreign> [and   
      <foreign lang="ar">مِنْ <ref cref="n30864-2" target="عَهْدِهِ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>], meaning <hi rend="ital">I am clear of responsibility to thee for any fault that thou mayest find in this slave known to exist in him while he was with me.</hi> (AHeyth, Mgh, TA.) See 4. And you say also, <foreign lang="ar">عُهْدَتُهُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">عَلَى فُلَانٍ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The responsibility for the rectification of any fault that may be found in him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, is upon such a one.</hi> (S, * Mgh, Msb, * K, * TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">فِى الأَمْرِ عُهْدَةٌ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">In the affair is an occasion for reverting to it for the purpose of its rectification;</hi> (Msb;) i. e. <hi rend="ital">the affair is not yet performed soundly, thoroughly,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">well,</hi> (S, O, Msb,) <hi rend="ital">and the manager thereof has to revert to it in order to render it so.</hi> (Msb.)                   <hi rend="ital">In it is a fault, a defect,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">an imperfection.</hi> (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">فِى عَقْلِهِ عُهْدَةٌ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">In his intellect is a weakness.</hi> (S, A, O, K.) And <foreign lang="ar">فِى خَطِّهِ عُهْدَةٌ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">In his handwriting is a weakness:</hi> (K:) or <hi rend="ital">badness:</hi> (A:) or <hi rend="ital">faulty formation of the letters.</hi> (O.)       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  See also <foreign lang="ar">عَهْدَةٌ</foreign>.    </entryFree>2c:T468,<entryFree id="n30868" key="عَهِيدٌ" type="main">
